name:Pâ€aâ€tâ€râ€iâ€câ€k
info:Elegant Queen Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Couples
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted December 4, 2023
msg:I chose Atour S Hotel for this trip to Lanzhou, because Atour Hotel is a leader in the entire hotel industry; and it did not disappoint my expectations of Atour Hotel this time;
Advantages;
1. The price-performance ratio is extremely high. The overall price of the hotel is not expensive, but the overall service provided by the hotel at this price is beyond the price itself;
2. The hotel is located in Nanguan Cross, Lanzhou, which is the city center, and the hotel front desk is located on the 38th floor of Asia-Europe International, which provides better privacy for check-in. The hotel front desk check-in efficiency is very high, and it is also upgraded for free when checking in. Executive City View Room, three sides of floor-to-ceiling glass can better enjoy the night view of Lanzhou. From the hotel room, you can directly see the Yellow River and the Yellow River Iron Bridge, which is very ornamental; 
3. The hotel also provides evening porridge and snacks when checking in, but because we returned to the hotel late, we did not enjoy it, which is quite regrettable; after ordering takeout at the hotel, you must remember to write your room number into the delivery address. The hotel front desk lady will let the food delivery robot automatically deliver it to the door according to your room number, eliminating the trouble of going to the front desk to pick up the food. This also needs to be given a big thumbs up! ! 
4. The hotel room is very spacious. The design of separate toilet and bathtub also provides great convenience. The curtains and screens are electrically controlled and can be opened and closed with one button, which is also very technological. There are 3 modes for the control of room lighting at the bedside, namely sleep, bright (I forgot another mode). You can adjust to sleep mode with one button at night. In sleep mode, only the bedside a**osphere light is turned on. For me who needs a certain light source to sleep, it is a great convenience. There is also a mobile phone wireless charging plate at the bedside, which also provides excellent convenience. Before going to bed, you only need to throw the mobile phone on the wireless charging panel. 
5. The hotel's toiletries smell woody and very advanced. Because the climate in Lanzhou is relatively dry, the hotel's toiletries have a very good moisturizing effect. After taking a shower, both the hair and the body are moisturized. This also gives a big thumbs up to the selection of toiletries at Atour S Hotel; 
6. What surprised me most was the hotel's pillows. There are two types of pillows to choose from, one is memory latex (I forgot the other one). The memory latex pillow is so comfortable that the neck is very comfortable when sleeping, which greatly relieves the fatigue of the day;
7. The slippers provided by the hotel are also of excellent quality, making people want to take a few more pairs home (but I finally held back)
8. The hotel's bathrobe is the most comfortable among all the hotels I have stayed in (more comfortable than the five-star luxury hotels such as Four Seasons, Sheraton, Hilton, Shangri-La, etc.). This is what surprised me the most. I never thought that Atour's bathrobe would be so comfortable that I didn't want to take it off after putting it on. The fabric is soft and very skin-friendly. The overall bathrobe is also very design-conscious. It is not only warm but also very stylish after putting it on;
9. The hotel has a very good location. There is a Ma Youbu beef noodle restaurant within 100 meters downstairs. You don't have to run far to eat authentic Lanzhou beef noodles; it is within a 10-minute walk from Zhengning Road Snack Street, which is very convenient!
There are too many advantages to list, so I will just list these first. I hope that these advantages will be maintained and passed on by Atour S Hotel;

Next, I will talk about a few things that I think can be done better:
Points worth improving:
1. The air conditioning and heating of the hotel cannot be adjusted automatically, and the room will be a bit stuffy at night, but it is not a big problem. For the winter weather in Lanzhou, this temperature is still quite comfortable;
2. The hair dryer in the hotel is actually the "Zhibai" brand. I have been using this brand at home, but there is a situation where the hair dryer cannot be turned on after using it for a period of time due to overheating protection. This is quite embarrassing. After all, after my wife blows her hair, I can't use it. When using a hair dryer, you need to wait at least 2-3 minutes for the hair dryer to cool down naturally before you can use it;
3. There is an elevator from the first floor to the 38th floor, and another elevator from the 38th floor to the room. This design itself is very good and has privacy, but the elevator from the first floor to the 38th floor runs slowly, and you often need to wait for a while on the 38th floor before you can take the elevator to the first floor;

Overall, this stay experience is excellent. Atour S Hotel completely exceeded my expectations and provided services and various facilities comparable to five-star hotels. Next time I come to Lanzhou, I will definitely choose Atour S Hotel. I hope Atour S Hotel will get better and better! !

If the full score is 10, I will give 9.8 points, and the remaining 0.2 points look forward to your improvement! !
----------------------------------------
